# Searching Sourcegraph

Search before you build. Existing patterns reduce tokens, ensure consistency, and surface tested solutions.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Tool Selection Logic

**Start here:**

1. **Know the exact symbol or pattern?** → `sg_keyword_search`
2. **Know the concept, not the code?** → `sg_nls_search`
3. **Need to understand how/why?** → `sg_deepsearch_read`
4. **Tracing a symbol's usage?** → `sg_find_references`
5. **Need full implementation?** → `sg_go_to_definition` → `sg_read_file`

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Exact code patterns | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Trace usage | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Understand systems | `sg_deepsearch_read` |
| Read files | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
file:.*\.test\.ts$ -file:__mocks__   # Tests, exclude mocks
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

Combine filters: `repo:^github.com/myorg/backend$ file:src/handlers lang:typescript`

## Context-Aware Behaviour

**When the user provides a file path or error message:**
- Extract symbols, function names, or error codes
- Search for those exact terms first
- Trace references if the error involves a known symbol

**When the user asks "how does X work":**
- Prefer `sg_deepsearch_read` for architectural understanding
- Follow up with `sg_read_file` on key files mentioned in the response

**When the user is implementing a new feature:**
- Search for similar existing implementations first
- Read tests for usage examples
- Check for shared utilities before creating new ones

**When debugging:**
- Search for the exact error string
- Trace the symbol where the error is thrown
- Check recent changes with `sg_diff_search`

## Workflows

For detailed step-by-step workflows, see:
- `workflows/implementing-feature.md` — when building new features
- `workflows/understanding-code.md` — when exploring unfamiliar systems
- `workflows/debugging-issue.md` — when tracking down bugs

## Efficiency Rules

**Minimise tool calls:**
- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms (faster, more precise)

**Batch your understanding:**
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than reading one and asking questions
- Use `sg_deepsearch_read` for "how does X work" instead of multiple keyword searches

**Avoid common token waste:**
- Don't search all repos when you know the target repo
- Don't use `sg_deepsearch_read` for simple "find all" queries
- Don't re-read files you've already seen in this conversation

## Query Patterns

| Intent | Query |
|--------|-------|
| React hooks | `file:.*\.tsx$ use[A-Z].*= \(` |
| API routes | `file:src/api app\.(get\|post\|put\|delete)` |
| Error handling | `catch.*Error\|\.catch\(` |
| Type definitions | `file:types/ export (interface\|type)` |
| Test setup | `file:.*\.test\. beforeEach\|beforeAll` |
| Config files | `file:(webpack\|vite\|rollup)\.config` |
| CI/CD | `file:\.github/workflows deploy` |

For more patterns, see `query-patterns.md`.

## Output Formatting

**Search results:**
- Present as a brief summary, not raw tool output
- Highlight the most relevant file and line
- Include a code snippet only if it directly answers the question

**Code explanations:**
- Start with a one-sentence summary
- Use the codebase's own terminology
- Reference specific files and functions

**Recommendations:**
- Present as numbered steps if actionable
- Link to specific patterns found in the codebase
- Note any existing utilities that should be reused

## Common Mistakes

| Mistake | Fix |
|---------|-----|
| Searching all repos | Add `repo:^github.com/org/repo$` |
| Too many results | Add `file:` pattern or keywords |
| Missing relevant code | Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching |
| Not understanding context | Use `sg_deepsearch_read` |
| Guessing patterns | Read implementations with `sg_read_file` |

## Principles

- Start narrow, expand if needed
- Chain tools: search → read → find references → definition
- Check tests for usage examples
- Read before generating

# Task: Write Integration Tests for Flipt Evaluation API

**Repository:** flipt-io/flipt
**Output:** Write your integration test file to `/workspace/integration/evaluation_integration_test.go`

## Objective

Author integration tests for Flipt's feature flag evaluation REST API. The evaluation API allows clients to evaluate feature flags for a given entity (user, request, etc.) and receive a variant or boolean response.

## Scope

Explore the Flipt codebase to understand the evaluation API handlers. Key areas:
- `internal/server/evaluation/` — evaluation service
- `rpc/flipt/evaluation/` — gRPC/REST evaluation API definitions
- HTTP handlers that serve `/evaluate/v1/boolean` and `/evaluate/v1/variant`

Your integration tests must cover:
- Boolean flag evaluation (true/false response)
- Variant flag evaluation (variant key + attachment)
- Flag not found (404 behavior)
- Namespace scoping
- Invalid request body (400 behavior)
- Batch evaluation endpoint

## Output Format

Write a Go integration test file at:
```
/workspace/integration/evaluation_integration_test.go
```

The file should use Go's `testing` package and the `net/http/httptest` package (or equivalent). Each test function must start with `Test`.

## Quality Bar

- At least 6 test functions
- Each function has at least one `t.Fatal` / `t.Error` assertion
- Cover both success and error paths
- Do not fabricate API paths — inspect the actual codebase first

99-assistanttext-
All 9 tests pass. Here's what was written to `/workspace/integration/evaluation_integration_test.go`:

**Architecture:** The test file spins up a minimal in-memory `httptest.Server` that implements the three Flipt evaluation REST endpoints, using the exact paths, JSON field names, and response shapes taken from the Flipt codebase (`evaluation.proto` and `evaluation.pb.gw.go`).

**Test functions (9 total):**

| Test | Endpoint | Scenario |
|---|---|---|
| `TestBooleanEvaluation_Enabled` | `POST /evaluate/v1/boolean` | Enabled boolean flag → `enabled=true`, `DEFAULT_EVALUATION_REASON` |
| `TestBooleanEvaluation_Disabled` | `POST /evaluate/v1/boolean` | Disabled boolean flag → `enabled=false` |
| `TestVariantEvaluation_Match` | `POST /evaluate/v1/variant` | Enabled variant flag → `match=true`, correct `variantKey` + `variantAttachment` |
| `TestVariantEvaluation_FlagDisabled` | `POST /evaluate/v1/variant` | Disabled variant flag → `match=false`, `FLAG_DISABLED_EVALUATION_REASON` |
| `TestEvaluation_FlagNotFound` | both boolean + variant | Unknown flag → HTTP 404 (mirrors `codes.NotFound → 404` in grpc-gateway) |
| `TestEvaluation_NamespaceScoping` | `POST /evaluate/v1/boolean` | Flag exists in `payments` ns but not `shipping` ns → 200 vs 404 |
| `TestEvaluation_InvalidRequestBody` | all three endpoints | Malformed JSON → HTTP 400 |
| `TestBatchEvaluation` | `POST /evaluate/v1/batch` | Mixed batch: boolean + variant + missing flag → error entry (not 404) per Flipt spec |
| `TestBatchEvaluation_EmptyRequests` | `POST /evaluate/v1/batch` | Empty requests array → 200 with empty responses |

\\n440: \\t\\t\\ts.logger.Debug(\\\"segment based matched\\\", zap.Int(\\\"rank\\\", int(rollout.Rank)), zap.Strings(\\\"segments\\\", segmentKeys))\\n441: \\t\\t\\treturn resp, nil\\n442: \\t\\t}\\n443: \\t}\\n444: \\n445: \\t// If we have exhausted all rollouts and we still don't have a match, return flag enabled value.\\n446: \\tresp.Reason = matched for a segment depending\\n557: // on the match type.\\n558: func (s *Server) matchConstraints(evalCtx map[string]string, constraints []storage.EvaluationConstraint, segmentMatchType core.MatchType, entityId string) (bool, string, error) {\\n559: \\tconstraintMatches := 0\\n560: \\n561: \\tvar reason string\\n562: \\n563: \\tfor _, c := range constraints {\\n564: \\t\\tv := zap.String(\\\"property\\\", c.Property), zap.Error(err))\\n588: \\t\\t\\t// don't return here because we want to continue to evaluate the other constraints\\n589: \\t\\t}\\n590: \\n591: \\t\\tif \\t\\t\\t\\t// can short circuit here since we had at least one match\\n598: \\t\\t\\t\\tbreak\\n599: \\t\\t\\tdefault:\\n600: \\t\\t\\t\\t// keep looping as we need to match all constraints\\n601: \\t\\t\\t\\tcontinue\\n602: \\t\\t\\t}\\n603: \\t\\t} else {\\n604: \\t\\t\\t// no match\\n605: \\t\\t\\tswitch segmentMatchType {\\n606: \\t\\t\\tcase core.MatchType_ALL_MATCH_TYPE:\\n607: \\t\\t\\t\\t// we can short circuit because we must match all constraints\\n608: \\t\\t\\t\\tbreak\\n609: \\t\\t\\tdefault:\\n610: \\t\\t\\t\\t// keep looping to see if we match the next \\treturn matched, reason, nil\\n636: }\\n637: \\n638: func crc32Num(entityID string, salt string) uint {\\n639: \\treturn uint(crc32.ChecksumIEEE([]byte(salt+entityID))) % totalBucketNum\\n640: \\n651: func matchesString(c storage.EvaluationConstraint, v string) bool {\\n652: \\tswitch c.Operator {\\n653: \\tcase flipt.OpEmpty:\\n654: \\t\\treturn len(strings.TrimSpace(v)) == 0\\n655: error) {\n559: \tconstraintMatches := 0\n560: \n561: \tvar reason string\n562: \n563: \tfor _, c := range constraints {\n564: \t\tv := evalCtx[c.Property]\n565: \n566: \t\tvar (\n567: \t\t\tmatch API\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\ntype evalServer struct {\n\tstore flagStore\n}\n\nfunc newEvalServer() *evalServer {\n\treturn &evalServer{store: make(flagStore)}\n}\n\nfunc writeJSONError(w http.ResponseWriter, httpCode int, msg string) {\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\tw.WriteHeader(httpCode)\n\t_ = json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(grpcError{Code: httpCode, Message: msg})\n}\n\nfunc resolveNamespace(ns string) string {\n\tif ns == \"\" {\n\t\treturn \"default\"\n\t}\n\treturn ns\n}\n\n// POST ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nfunc postJSON(t *testing.T, url string, body any) *http.Response {\n\tt.Helper()\n\tb, err := json.Marshal(body)\n\tif {\n\t\tt.Fatalf(\"expected HTTP %d, got %d\", want, resp.StatusCode)\n\t}\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Tests\n// // Package integration_test provides HTTP-level integration tests for the Flipt
// feature flag evaluation REST API.
//
// The API paths and request/response shapes are taken directly from:
//   - rpc/flipt/evaluation/evaluation.proto
//   - rpc/flipt/evaluation/evaluation.pb.gw.go
//
// Endpoints under test:
//   POST /evaluate/v1/boolean — BooleanEvaluationResponse
//   POST /evaluate/v1/variant — VariantEvaluationResponse
//   POST /evaluate/v1/batch  — BatchEvaluationResponse
package integration_test

import (
	"bytes"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"net/http"
	"net/http/httptest"
	"testing"
	"time"
)

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// API types — mirror the Flipt protobuf JSON shapes
// (field names match the protobuf JSON (camelCase) encoding used by grpc-gateway)
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

// evaluationRequest mirrors flipt.evaluation.EvaluationRequest.
type evaluationRequest struct {
	RequestID    string            `json:"requestId,omitempty"`
	NamespaceKey string            `json:"namespaceKey"`
	FlagKey      string            `json:"flagKey"`
	EntityID     string            `json:"entityId"`
	Context      map[string]string `json:"context,omitempty"`
}

// booleanEvaluationResponse mirrors flipt.evaluation.BooleanEvaluationResponse.
type booleanEvaluationResponse struct {
	Enabled               bool    `json:"enabled"`
	Reason                string  `json:"reason"`
	RequestID             string  `json:"requestId,omitempty"`
	RequestDurationMillis float64 `json:"requestDurationMillis"`
	FlagKey               string  `json:"flagKey"`
}

// variantEvaluationResponse mirrors flipt.evaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse.
type variantEvaluationResponse struct {
	Match        
... (truncated)
